		<p style="margin:0pt;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;text-align:center;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 12pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;text-transform:uppercase;color:#6E3F28;font-size:12pt;">Chipotle ANNOUNCES THIRD QUARTER 2021 RESULTS</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;text-align:center;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 12pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;text-transform:uppercase;color:#6E3F28;font-size:12pt;">RECORD QUARTERLY SALES DRIVEN BY COMPARABLE restaurant SALES increasing 15.1%</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;border-bottom:1pt solid #996633 ;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 12pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;text-transform:uppercase;color:#6E3F28;font-size:12pt;">&#xFEFF;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">NEWPORT BEACH, Calf. &#x2013; October 21, 2021 &#x2013; Chipotle Mexican Grill, Inc. (NYSE: CMG) today reported financial results for its third quarter ended September 30, 2021.</font>
		</p>

Excluding a $0.16 after-tax net impact resulting from a </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">tax benefit</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">, which was partially offset by</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> certain</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">stock compensation </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">expenses, corporate restructuring</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> costs</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">, restaurant asset impairment and closure costs, </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">and</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">certain </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">other </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">expenses</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">, adjusted diluted earnings per share was $7.02, an 86.7% increase from $3.76</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;font-size:5pt;vertical-align:super;line-height:100%"> &nbsp;1</font></p></td></tr></table></div>

			<a name="_Hlk53554988"></a><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">&#x201C;Chipotle&#x2019;s </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">third</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> quarter results </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">demonstrate strong momentum in our business fueled by a multi-pronged strategy and a passionate team that&#x2019;s delighted to welcome more guests back into our restaurants</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">," said Brian Niccol, Chairman and CEO, Chipotle. "</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">Our team has proven their ability to be resilient and successfully execute against macro complexities. As a result, I believe we are better positioned to drive sustainable long-term growth than ever before, which makes me excited about what we can accomplish in the years ahead</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">.&#x201D;</font>

			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">The health and well-being of our employees and guests continues to be our top priority. Beyond the investments made in our people, restaurants</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">,</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> and </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">s</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">upply chain, we are closely following the recommendations of the CDC and local health departm</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">ents. We have implemented and enhanced numerous protocols that</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> give our employees and guests confidence that Chipotle remains steadfast in our commitment to keep them safe as in-restaurant </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">ordering and </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">dining</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> increases</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">.</font>

We also have access to a</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> &nbsp;$</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">5</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">00 million untapped credit facility. Our financial strength gives us the opportunity to make on-going strategic investments in our people, business, and communities, which we believe will benefit us for years to come. </font>

</div>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;;font-size: 10pt"><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">Results for the three months ended </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">September</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">30</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">, 202</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">1</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">: &nbsp;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">Revenue in the </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">thir</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">d quarter was $</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">2.0</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> billion, an increase of </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">21.9</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">% compared to the </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">third</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> quarter of 2020 and includes a 1</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">5</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">.</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">1</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">% increase in comparable restaurant sales. We believe on-going strength in digital sales</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">, the strong recovery of in-restaurant sales, and positive customer reception to our new menu items </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">contributed to </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">the strong</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> revenue growth. For Q</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">4</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">, &nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">while uncertainty remains on several fronts including the potential impact of COVID-19 as well as inflationary and staffing pressures, we&#x2019;re encouraged by our strong underlying </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">business momentum and if this trend continues, we expect our comparable restaurant sales to be in the low to mid double-digits</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> range.</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> This assumes about 200 basis points less pricing contribution during the fourth quarter versus the third quarter as we lap some of our delivery menu price increases, and our brisket limited time offer will be for a partial quarter this year as compared to the full quarter of carne asada last year.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">Digital sales grew </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">8.6</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">% year over year to $</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">840.4</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> million and represented 4</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">2.</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">8% of sales. A little more than half of the digital sales were from order ahead transactions as guests increasingly appreciate both the convenience </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">and value </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">offered by this channel, as well as the added convenience of more Chipotlanes.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">We opened </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">41</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> new restaurants during the </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">third</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> quarter including </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">two</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> relocation</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">s</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">, bringing the total restaurant count to </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">2,8</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">92</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">. During the quarter, </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">36</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> of the </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">41</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> new restaurants included a Chipotlane. These formats continue to perform very well and are helping enhance guest access and convenience, as well as increase new restaurant sa</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">les, margins, and </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">returns. </font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">Food, beverage and packaging costs in the third quarter were 30.3% of revenue, a decrease of 200 basis points compared to the third quarter of 2020. The decrease was </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">due </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">primarily to </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">leverage from </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">menu price increases, partially offset by higher costs, most notably beef and freight</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">.</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">Restaurant level operating margin was 23.5%, an increase from 19.5% in the third quarter of 2020. The improvement was driven primarily by leverage from comparable restaurant sales including menu price increases, partially offset by </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">wage inflation and </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">higher </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">costs associated with beef and </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">freight</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">General and administrative expenses for the third quarter were $14</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">6.0</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> million on a GAAP basis, or $136.</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">8</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> million on a non-GAAP basis</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">, excluding $7.6 million for a </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">COVID-19 related </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">modification </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">made in December 2020 </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">to </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">our </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">2018 performance shares, $1.5 million of transformation expenses, and $0.</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">1</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> million of</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> certain other </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">expenses. GAAP and non-GAAP general and administrative expenses for the </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">third</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> quarter of 2021 also include </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">$99.8 million of </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">underlying general and administrative expenses</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">, $27.8 million of non-cash stock compensation, $8.5 million related to higher bonus accruals as well as payroll taxes on equity vesting and stock option exercises, and $0.6 million related to our upcoming all-manager conference. </font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">The GAAP effective income tax rate for the third quarter was 14.7%, which is lower than our expected effective income tax rate for the full year 2021, due to elevated excess tax benefits related to option exercises and equity vesting </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">and a return to provision tax benefit </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">from </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">a &nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">net operating loss generated</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> on our 2020 federal income tax return and carried back to prior years that was</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> recorded in the third quarter</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">. On a non-GAAP basis, the 2021 third quarter effective tax rate was 19.7%.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">Net income for the third quarter was $204.4 million, or $7.18 per diluted share, an increase from $80.2 million, or $2.82 per diluted share, in the third quarter of 2020. Excluding the impact of a tax benefit, PSU modification expenses, corporate restructuring expenses, </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">and </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">restaurant asset impairment and closure costs, adjusted net income was $199.</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">8</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> million and adjusted diluted earnings per share was</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> $7.02.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">During the quarter, our Board of Directors approved the investment of up to an additional $100 million, exclusive of commissions, to repurchase shares of our common stock, subject to market conditions. Including this repurchase authorization, $209.8 million was available as of September 30, 2021. The repurchase authorization may be modified, suspended, or discontinued at any time. We repurchased $</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">98.7</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> million of stock at an average price per share of $</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">1,813</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> during the third quarter. </font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">More information will be available in our Quarterly Report on Form 10-Q, which will be filed with the SEC by the end of </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">October</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">.</font>
		</p>

			<a name="_Hlk74719682"></a><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">Restaurant level operating margin</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">represents total revenue less direct restaurant operating costs, expressed as a percent of total revenue.</font></p></td></tr></table></div>

			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">Chipotle</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">will</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> host a conference call to discuss </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">third</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> quarter 202</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">1</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> financial results on </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">Thurs</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">day, </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">October 21</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">, 202</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">1</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">, at 4:30 PM Eastern time.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">The</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">conference</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> call can be accessed live over the phone by dialing 1-888-317-6003 or for international callers by dialing 1-412-317-6061 and use code: </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">1417737</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">. An archived webcast will be available approximately one hour after the end of the call.</font>

		<p style="margin:13.5pt 0pt 0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">About Chipotle</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">Chipotle Mexican Grill, Inc. (NYSE: CMG) is cultivating a better world by serving responsibly sourced, classically-cooked, real food with wholesome ingredients without artificial colors, flavors or preservatives. Chipotle had </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">nearly</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> 2,</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">90</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">0 restaurants as of </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">September 30</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">, 202</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">1</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">, in the United States, Canada, the United Kingdom, France and Germany and is the only restaurant company of its size that owns and operates all its restaurants. </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">Chipotle is ranked on the Fortune 500 and is recognized on the 2021 lists for Forbes&#x2019; America&#x2019;s Best Employers and Fortune&#x2019;s Most Admired Companies. </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">With </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">nearly 95,000 em</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">ployees passionate about providing a great guest experience, Chipotle is a longtime leader and innovator in the fo</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">od industry. Chipotle is committed to making its food more accessible to everyone while continuing to be a brand with a demonstrated purpose as it leads the way in digital, technology and sustainable business practices. For more information or to place an order online, visit </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;text-transform:uppercase;color:#C08C19;background-color: #FFFFFF;">WWW.CHIPOTLE.COM</font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">.</font>
		</p>

the increasingly competitive labor market and </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;">changes in the availability and cost of labor</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;">; the financial impact of increasing our average hourly wage to $15.00; the impact of federal, state or local government regulations relating to our employees, employment practices, restaurant design and construction, and the sale of food or alcoholic beverages; our ability to achieve our planned growth, such as the availability of suitable new restaurant sites; increases in ingredient and other operating costs due to our Food With Integrity philosophy, tariffs or trade restrictions and supply shortages; the uncertainty of our ability to achieve expected levels of comparable restaurant sales due to factors such as changes in consumers' perceptions of our brand, including as a result of actual or rumored food safety concerns or other negative publicity, decreased overall consumer spending (including but not limited to the increase in unemployment caused by </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;">COVID-19</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;">), or the inability to increase menu prices or realize the benefits of menu price increases; 		<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 3pt;text-align:center;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-weight:bold;">RECONCILIATION OF NON-GAAP FINANCIAL MEASURES</font><font style="display: inline;font-weight:bold;">&nbsp;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:13pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<a name="_Hlk22568764"></a><font style="display: inline;">The following tables provide a reconciliation of non-GAAP financial measures presented in the text above to the most directly comparable financial measures calculated and presented in accordance with GAAP. </font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;">Adjusted net income is net income excluding expenses related to </font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">restaurant asset impairment, corporate restructuring, legal proceedings, stock-</font><font style="display: inline;">based compensation modification expense, and certain other costs. Adjusted general and administrative expense is general and administrative expense excluding transformation expenses, legal proceedings, stock-based compensation modification expense, and certain other costs. The non-GAAP effective tax rate is the effective tax rate adjusted to reflect the after tax impact of non-GAAP adjustments. Restaurant Level Operating Margin, a non-GAAP financial measure, is equal to the revenues generated by our restaurants less their direct operating costs which consist of food, beverage and packaging, labor, occupancy and other operating costs. This performance measure primarily includes the costs that restaurant level managers can directly control and excludes other operating costs that are essential to conduct our business. Management uses restaurant level operating margin as a measure of restaurant performance. Management believes restaurant level operating margin is useful to investors in that it highlights trends in our core business that may not otherwise be apparent to investors when relying solely on GAAP financial measures. We present these non-GAAP measures in order to facilitate meaningful evaluation of our operating performance across periods. These adjustments are intended to provide greater transparency of underlying performance and to allow investors to evaluate our business on the same basis as our management, which uses these non-GAAP measures in evaluating the company&#x2019;s performance. Our adjusted net income, adjusted diluted earnings per share, adjusted general and administrative expenses, non-GAAP effective tax rate and restaurant level operating margin measures may not be comparable to other companies&#x2019; adjusted measures. These adjustments are not necessarily indicative of what our actual financial performance would have been during the periods presented and should be viewed in addition to, and not as an alternative to, our results prepared in accordance with GAAP. Further details regarding these adjustments are included in the tables below.</font>
		</p>
